remarks:        I.IV.  MED adjustment
remarks:
remarks:        Default MED is 0 for originated prefixes (origin AS = peer AS), 10 for all others
remarks:
remarks:        For originated prefixes:
remarks:        31500:1005 - Set med 05
remarks:        31500:1010 - Set med 10
remarks:        31500:1015 - Set med 15
remarks:        31500:10   - Accept med as-is, do not set
remarks:
remarks:        For non-originated prefixes:
remarks:        31500:1015 - Set med 15
remarks:        31500:1020 - Set med 20
remarks:        31500:1030 - Set med 30

remarks:        II. Global IX
remarks:
remarks:        ------------------------------------------------
remarks:        > Routing and peering issue: noc@gnm.net
remarks:        > Customer's support:        noc@gnm.net
remarks:        > Spam abuse:                abuse@gnm.net
remarks:        ------------------------------------------------
remarks:
remarks:        AS-SET: AS-GLOBAL-IX
remarks:

remarks:
remarks:        II.II.  Traffic management communities:
remarks:
remarks:        0:<peer-as>           - Do not announce prefix to a peer with AS <peer-as>
remarks:        31500:<peer-as>       - Announce prefix to a peer with AS <peer-as>
remarks:        0:<city-community>    - Do not announce prefix to a peers with <city-community>
remarks:        0:<segment-community> - Do not announce prefix to a peers with <segment-community>
remarks:        0:31500               - Do not announce prefix to anyone
remarks:        0:666                 - Blackhole community (/32 prefixes only)
remarks:        31500:31500           - Announce prefix to everyone (default)
remarks:        31500:0               - Set local preference 0
remarks:        31500:50              - Set local preference 50
remarks:        31500:80              - Set local preference 80
remarks:
remarks:
